Template Generation (per CPU)\nEach architecture has a `TemplateInterpreterGenerator` that JIT-generates native code:\n- x86: `templateInterpreterGenerator_x86.cpp`, `_x86_32.cpp`, `_x86_64.cpp`\n- aarch64: `templateInterpreterGenerator_aarch64.cpp`\n- riscv: `templateInterpreterGenerator_riscv.cpp`\n- ppc: `templateInterpreterGenerator_ppc.cpp`\n- s390: `templateInterpreterGenerator_s390.cpp`\n- arm: `templateInterpreterGenerator_arm.cpp`\n\n### 3. Dispatch Mechanism (InterpreterMacroAssembler per CPU)\nEach architecture implements `dispatch_base()`, `dispatch_only()`, `dispatch_next()` in their `interp_masm_*.cpp` files, plus `templateTable_*.cpp` for bytecode handler implementations.\n\n### 4.
